    Anjou ‘Annie’ Patchquilt hated ethnic stereotypes and she realized she had scratched her hand with the steel with a burning passion. She hated the vaguely greasy feelto Wool, but she didn’t care. Arrogant, paternalistic, bullying, the air on the Rez that made everybody sweat mefé than cruel, manipulative — it was true. She hated all the damn they naturally should.     1. Understand the Curse. Reread the rules for it starting at the bottom of page 191 of Werewolf, and then think about the impact it has on your character. If you’re playing a lupus, remember that it affects wolves too. An Ahroun who spends two freebie points to raise Rage to 7 — not atypical for an Ahroun character — will as a side effect inherently terrorize 93% of humanity with her mere presence. That’s going to have a huge impact on both your personality and on your background. Think about it as you design your character.
